#off

#cheat Teleport To And Back V1
//ID: 19758
//Score: 4
//Author: emcp
//Category: Teleport
//Description: This cheat allows you to teleport to a specified location by pressing R + up and then by pressing R + down you can return to the location you were when you first teleported
//
//after each teleport you have to turn the cheat back on this is to stop constant teleporting in the cheat device (if theres a way around this please tell me thanks)
//
//this is useful if you make a construction like a hide away and you are being chased by police you can cool down in the hideaway and return back to the spot you were
//
//this is the first version i dont think it works in cars that will work very very soon and more features
//
//EDITED BY: Durka Durka Mahn on 07/06/07 19:05:01 Fixed!
//
//EDITED BY: Durka Durka Mahn on 09/06/07 03:27:54
//Image: none
//Time: 07/06/2007 18:52:05
//Working: Yes
//My First Cheat Created For VCS
//Created By Emmet Mc Poland (emcp)
if(press & CTRL_UP && buttons & CTRL_RTRIGGER)
{
x = getfloat(pobj+ 0x30);
y = getfloat(pobj + 0x34);
z = getfloat(pobj+ 0x38); 
}
if(press & CTRL_DOWN && buttons & CTRL_RTRIGGER) {
setfloat(pobj+0x30, x, y, z);
}

#cheat Custom Gravity
//ID: 19757
//Score: 13
//Author: Durka Durka Mahn
//Category: Player
//Description: Use the D-Pad to change the gravity along the X/Y axi.
//Image: none
//Time: 07/06/2007 01:23:42
//Working: Yes
gravity = 0.002;
static speed;
static menu;
if(press & CTRL_RIGHT) {
	menu = 1;
	speed = 0;
}
if(press & CTRL_LEFT) {
	menu = 2;
	speed = 0;
}
if(press & CTRL_UP) {
	menu = 3;
	speed = 0;
}
if(press & CTRL_DOWN) {
	menu = 4;
	speed = 0;
}
if(menu == 1) {
	if(!getint(pobj+0x150)) {
		speed += gravity;
		setfloat(pobj+0x30, getfloat(pobj+0x30) + speed);
	} else {
		speed = 0;
	}
}
if(menu == 2) {
	if(!getint(pobj+0x150)) {
		speed -= gravity;
		setfloat(pobj+0x30, getfloat(pobj+0x30) + speed);
	} else {
		speed = 0;
	}
}
if(menu == 3) {
	if(!getint(pobj+0x150)) {
		speed += gravity;
		setfloat(pobj+0x34, getfloat(pobj+0x34) + speed);
	} else {
		speed = 0;
	}
}
if(menu == 4) {
	if(!getint(pobj+0x150)) {
		speed -= gravity;
		setfloat(pobj+0x34, getfloat(pobj+0x34) + speed);
	} else {
		speed = 0;
	}
} 
setshort(0x08e90bd8, 1, 'U', 's', 'e', ' ', 't', 'h', 'e', ' ', 'D', '-', 'P', 'a', 'd', ' ', 't', 'o', ' ', 'c', 'h', 'a', 'n', 'g', 'e', ' ', 'y', 

'o', 'u', 'r', ' ', 'G', 'r', 'a', 'v', 'i', 't', 'y', '!', 0);

#cheat max out bullets that hit stat
//ID: 19776
//Score: 1
//Author: creepers
//Category: Player Stats
//Description: lol,first cheat
//
//EDITED BY: psphacker108 on 15/06/07 04:42:19
//Image: none
//Time: 14/06/2007 12:02:20

static init;

{
  lasttime = getchar( 0x08bb3b41 );
  init = 1;
}
if( lasttime != getchar( 0x08bb3b41 ) )
{
  Nos -= 0.198;
  timepassed++;
  lasttime = getchar( 0x08bb3b41 );
}
if( timepassed < time )
{
   going = 1;
}
else {
 On = 0;
 timepassed = 0;
 going = 0;
}
}
if(going) {
  setchar(0x09569B90,    0x10);
  setchar(0x09569B94,    R,    G,    B);
  speed = 1.5;                                                                                  
  thrust = speed * 0.00333;      
  if(buttons & CTRL_CROSS) {                            
     setfloat(pcar + 0x0140,    getfloat(pcar + 0x0140) + getfloat(pcar + 0x0010) * thrust);          
     setfloat(pcar + 0x0144,    getfloat(pcar + 0x0144) + getfloat(pcar + 0x0014) * thrust);
  }
}
else
{
  boost = 0;
  setchar(0x09569B90,    0x4);
  setchar(0x09569B94,    63,    63,    63);
}
}

#cheat monster quad
//garage information//
setint(0x08C739B0,  230); //vehicle identifier
setchar(0x08C739d4, 0, 0, 0, 255); //vehicle base color RGB values
setchar(0x08C739d8,  255, 255, 255, 255); //vehicle stripe color RGB values
//suspension information//
setfloat(0x9631d60+0x74, 0.6); //suspension force
setfloat(0x9631d60+0x78, 5); //suspension damping
setfloat(0x9631d60+0x7c, 0); //upper limit
setfloat(0x9631d60+0x80, -0.75); //lower limit
setfloat(0x9631d60+0x84, 0.5); //bias
setfloat(0x9631d60+0x88, 1); //anti-dive
//tire information//
setfloat(0x9367f18, 1.35, 1.35); //wheel size
setfloat(0x9631d60+0xc4, 0.75); //traction loss
setfloat(0x9631d60+0x70, 0.50); //traction bias
setfloat(0x9631d60+0x6c, 0.95); //traction multiplier
//handling information//
setfloat(0x9631d60+0xbc, 6000); //mass
setfloat(0x9631d60+0xc0, 6000); //turn mass
setfloat(0x9631d60+0xa0, 0); //center of mass X
setfloat(0x9631d60+0xa4, 0); //center of mass Y
setfloat(0x9631d60+0xa8, -1.2); //center of mass Z
setfloat(0x9631d60+0x68, 35); //steering lock
setchar(0x9631d60+0x5c, '4', 'D', 4); //transmission data (drive type/engine type/# of gears)
off()

      if(p != pcar) setchar(p + 0x4c,  1);
 }
}

}

thrust = speed * 0.00333;                                    
setfloat(pcar + 0x0140,   getfloat(pcar + 0x0140) + getfloat(pcar + 0x0010) * thrust);          
setfloat(pcar + 0x0144,   getfloat(pcar + 0x0144) + getfloat(pcar + 0x0014) * thrust);

thrust = speed * 0.00333;
setchar(0x09569B90,   0x2);
setchar(0x09569B94,   255, 185, 50);

setfloat(pcar + 0x0144,   getfloat(pcar + 0x0144) + getfloat(pcar + 0x0014) * thrust);
}else{
setchar(0x09569B90,   0x4);
setchar(0x09569B94,   63, 63, 63);
}
}
